Applicable season: four seasons

product details:
1. Plain design: classic solid color design, simple and stylish temperament, timeless model, smooth line design, reflecting the big brand texture
2. Double-sided design: double-sided design, microfiber on both sides, soft and comfortable, beautiful and practical
3. Fluffy terry: Spiral terry is finer and tighter than ordinary bath towels, the surface is flat and greasy, the feel is light and rich, it does not fade or lose hair, it is dry and absorbent
4. Exquisite hemming: exquisite and elegant hemming design, tightly woven thread, the edges and corners are perfectly stitched without taking off the thread, durable and stylish
1. High water absorption: The ultra-fine fiber uses orange petal technology to divide the filament into eight petals, which increases the surface area of ??the fiber and increases the pores in the fabric. The capillary wicking effect is used to enhance the water absorption effect. Quickly absorb water and change quickly
Dryness becomes its distinctive feature.
2. Strong decontamination power: The fineness of microfibers with a diameter of 0.4m is only 1/10 of silk, and its special cross-section can more effectively capture dust particles as small as a few microns. The effect of decontamination and degreasing is very obvious.
3. Long life: due to the high strength and strong cutability of the ultrafine fiber, its service life is more than 4 times the service life of ordinary towels, and it is still invariable after multiple washings.
Molecular polymer fiber does not produce protein hydrolysis like cotton fiber, even if it is not dried after use, it will not mold, rot, and have a long life.
5. Easy to clean: When using ordinary towels, especially natural fiber towels, the dust, grease, dirt, etc. on the surface of the wiped object are directly absorbed into the fiber, and they remain in the fiber after use
Among them, it is not easy to remove, and it will even harden and lose its elasticity after being used for a long time, which affects the use. The ultra-fine fiber towel absorbs dirt between the fibers (not inside the fiber), plus the fiber has a high fiber density and high density, so the adsorption capacity is strong,
After use, just use clean water or a little detergent to clean.
6. No color fading: the dyeing process uses TF-215 and other dyes for ultra-fine fiber materials, and its retardation, migration, high temperature dispersibility, and decolorization indexes have reached the strict standards of the international export market, especially The advantage of not discoloring, so that it will not bring the trouble of discoloration and pollution when cleaning the surface of the article.",Light Purple,70*150CM,,,,CNY,91.19,0

3. Long life: due to the high strength and strong cutability of the ultrafine fiber, its service life is more than 4 times the service life of ordinary towels, and it is still invariable after multiple washings.
Molecular polymer fiber does not produce protein hydrolysis like cotton fiber, even if it is not dried after use, it will not mold, rot, and have a long life.
5. Easy to clean: When using ordinary towels, especially natural fiber towels, the dust, grease, dirt, etc. on the surface of the wiped object are directly absorbed into the fiber, and they remain in the fiber after use
Among them, it is not easy to remove, and it will even harden and lose its elasticity after being used for a long time, which affects the use. The ultra-fine fiber towel absorbs dirt between the fibers (not inside the fiber), plus the fiber has a high fiber density and high density, so the adsorption capacity is strong,
After use, just use clean water or a little detergent to clean.
6. No color fading: the dyeing process uses TF-215 and other dyes for ultra-fine fiber materials, and its retardation, migration, high temperature dispersibility, and decolorization indexes have reached the strict standards of the international export market, especially The advantage of not discoloring, so that it will not bring the trouble of discoloration and pollution when cleaning the surface of the article.",Orange,70*150CM,,,,CNY,91.19,0
